import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { creators } from '../data/creators';
import type { SignalRating } from '../types';
import { Shield, AlertTriangle, XCircle, Filter } from 'lucide-react';

const ratingConfig: Record<SignalRating, { label: string; icon: typeof Shield; className: string; bgClass: string }> = {
  GREEN: { label: 'Reliable', icon: Shield, className: 'text-accent-emerald', bgClass: 'bg-accent-emerald/10 border-accent-emerald/20' },
  YELLOW: { label: 'Mixed', icon: AlertTriangle, className: 'text-[var(--accent-amber)]', bgClass: 'bg-[var(--accent-amber)]/10 border-[var(--accent-amber)]/20' },
  RED: { label: 'Unreliable', icon: XCircle, className: 'text-[var(--accent-rose)]', bgClass: 'bg-[var(--accent-rose)]/10 border-[var(--accent-rose)]/20' },
};

const filterOptions: { key: string; label: string }[] = [
  { key: 'all', label: 'All' },
  { key: 'GREEN', label: '🟢 Reliable' },
  { key: 'YELLOW', label: '🟡 Mixed' },
  { key: 'RED', label: '🔴 Unreliable' },
];

export function SignalsPage() {
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all');

  const filtered = filter === 'all' ? creators : creators.filter((c) => c.rating === filter);

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-20">
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} className="mb-10">
        <h1 className="text-4xl sm:text-5xl font-bold text-foreground mb-4">Signal Watch</h1>
        <p className="text-muted-foreground text-lg mb-6">
          Credibility ratings for {creators.length} UAP & consciousness researchers.
          Not a judgment of character — a measure of sourcing rigor.
        </p>

        <div className="glass-cosmic rounded-xl p-4 flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-4 items-start sm:items-center">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            <Filter className="w-4 h-4" />
            <span>Filter:</span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {filterOptions.map((opt) => (
              <button
                key={opt.key}
                onClick={() => setFilter(opt.key)}
                className={`px-4 py-1.5 rounded-full text-sm font-medium transition-all ${
                  filter === opt.key
                    ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                    : 'bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-accent'
                }`}
              >
                {opt.label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>

      <div className="space-y-4">
        {filtered.map((c, i) => {
          const config = ratingConfig[c.rating];
          const Icon = config.icon;
          return (
            <motion.div
              key={c.id}
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              transition={{ delay: i * 0.06 }}
              className={`glass-cosmic rounded-xl p-6 border-l-4 ${config.bgClass}`}
            >
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4 mb-3">
                <div>
                  <h2 className="text-lg font-bold text-foreground">{c.name}</h2>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{c.platform}</p>
                </div>
                <div className={`flex items-center gap-1.5 text-sm font-semibold ${config.className} flex-shrink-0`}>
                  <Icon className="w-4 h-4" />
                  {config.label}
                </div>
              </div>
              <p className="text-sm text-foreground mb-3 leading-relaxed">{c.description}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground italic bg-secondary/30 rounded-lg px-3 py-2">{c.ratingNote}</p>
            </motion.div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { Telescope as TelescopeIcon, ChevronDown, ChevronUp, Sparkles, Info } from 'lucide-react';
import { EvidenceBadge } from '../components/EvidenceBadge';
import { telescopes } from '../data/telescopes';

type FilterType = 'all' | 'space' | 'ground';

export function TelescopePage() {
  const [typeFilter, setTypeFilter] = useState<FilterType>('all');
  const [expandedId, setExpandedId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const filtered = typeFilter === 'all' ? telescopes : telescopes.filter(t => t.type === typeFilter);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen py-16 px-4">
      <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto">
        <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} className="text-center mb-12">
          <TelescopeIcon className="w-12 h-12 text-primary mx-auto mb-4" />
          <h1 className="text-4xl sm:text-5xl font-bold text-foreground mb-3">Telescope Observatory</h1>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            From Hubble to James Webb — every major telescope, their groundbreaking discoveries year by year,
            and connections to anomalous phenomena.
          </p>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Type Filter */}
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mb-10">
          {(['all', 'space', 'ground'] as FilterType[]).map(f => (
            <button
              key={f}
              onClick={() => setTypeFilter(f)}
              className={`px-4 py-1.5 rounded-full text-sm font-medium capitalize transition-colors ${
                typeFilter === f
                  ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                  : 'glass-cosmic text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
              }`}
            >
              {f === 'all' ? 'All' : f === 'space' ? '🛰 Space' : '📡 Ground'}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Cards Grid */}
        <div className="space-y-6">
          <AnimatePresence mode="popLayout">
            {filtered.map((t, i) => {
              const isExpanded = expandedId === t.id;
              return (
                <motion.div
                  key={t.id}
                  layout
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                  exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
                  transition={{ delay: i * 0.06 }}
                >
                  <div className="glass-cosmic rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
                    {/* Header with Image */}
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setExpandedId(isExpanded ? null : t.id)}
                      className="w-full text-left"
                    >
                      <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row">
                        {/* Telescope Image */}
                        <div className="relative w-full sm:w-56 h-44 sm:h-auto shrink-0 overflow-hidden">
                          <img
                            src={t.image}
                            alt={t.name}
                            loading="lazy"
                            className="w-full h-full object-cover"
                          />
                          <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent to-[rgba(15,10,40,0.8)] hidden sm:block" />
                          <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-t from-[rgba(15,10,40,0.8)] to-transparent sm:hidden" />
                          {/* Status badge on image */}
                          <div className={`absolute top-3 left-3 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-bold ${
                            t.status === 'active' ? 'bg-emerald-500/20 text-emerald-400 border border-emerald-500/30' :
                            t.status === 'retired' ? 'bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-400 border border-amber-500/30' :
                            'bg-red-500/20 text-red-400 border border-red-500/30'
                          }`}>
                            {t.status.toUpperCase()}
                          </div>
                        </div>

                        {/* Info */}
                        <div className="flex-1 p-5">
                          <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                            <div className="flex-1">
                              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap mb-2">
                                <span className="text-2xl">{t.icon}</span>
                                <h3 className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground">{t.name}</h3>
                                <EvidenceBadge grade={t.grade} />
                              </div>
                              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-3">
                                <span className="font-mono bg-secondary px-2 py-0.5 rounded">{t.launchYear}</span>
                                <span className="capitalize">{t.type}-based</span>
                                <span>{t.discoveries.length} discoveries</span>
                              </div>
                              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">{t.summary}</p>

                              {/* Specs row */}
                              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-3">
                                {t.specs.slice(0, 3).map((s, si) => (
                                  <span key={si} className="text-xs bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground px-2 py-0.5 rounded flex items-center gap-1">
                                    <Info className="w-3 h-3" /> {s}
                                  </span>
                                ))}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                            <div className="text-muted-foreground shrink-0 mt-1">
                              {isExpanded ? <ChevronUp className="w-5 h-5" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-5 h-5" />}
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </button>

                    <AnimatePresence>
                      {isExpanded && (
                        <motion.div
                          initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                          animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
                          exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                          className="overflow-hidden"
                        >
                          <div className="px-5 pb-6 space-y-4 border-t border-border pt-4">
                            {/* All specs */}
                            {t.specs.length > 3 && (
                              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                                {t.specs.slice(3).map((s, si) => (
                                  <span key={si} className="text-xs bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground px-2 py-0.5 rounded flex items-center gap-1">
                                    <Info className="w-3 h-3" /> {s}
                                  </span>
                                ))}
                              </div>
                            )}

                            <h4 className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground flex items-center gap-2">
                              <span className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full" style={{ background: t.accentColor }} />
                              Key Discoveries ({t.discoveries.length})
                            </h4>

                            <div className="relative">
                              <div className="absolute left-3 top-0 bottom-0 w-px" style={{ background: t.accentColor, opacity: 0.3 }} />
                              <div className="space-y-4">
                                {t.discoveries.map((d, di) => (
                                  <motion.div
                                    key={di}
                                    initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -10 }}
                                    animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                                    transition={{ delay: di * 0.05 }}
                                    className="flex gap-4 pl-8 relative"
                                  >
                                    <div
                                      className="absolute left-1.5 w-3 h-3 rounded-full border-2 border-background"
                                      style={{ background: t.accentColor, top: '0.25rem' }}
                                    />
                                    <div className="flex-1">
                                      <div className="flex items-baseline gap-2 mb-0.5">
                                        <span className="text-xs font-mono text-primary shrink-0">{d.year}</span>
                                        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">{d.title}</p>
                                      </div>
                                      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{d.description}</p>
                                      {d.significance && (
                                        <p className="text-xs mt-1 flex items-center gap-1" style={{ color: t.accentColor }}>
                                          <Sparkles className="w-3 h-3" /> {d.significance}
                                        </p>
                                      )}
                                    </div>
                                  </motion.div>
                                ))}
                              </div>
                            </div>

                            {t.anomalyConnections && (
                              <div className="bg-accent rounded-lg p-4 mt-3 border border-primary/20">
                                <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-accent-neon mb-1">⚡ Anomaly Connection</p>
                                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{t.anomalyConnections}</p>
                              </div>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </motion.div>
                      )}
                    </AnimatePresence>
                  </div>
                </motion.div>
              );
            })}
          </AnimatePresence>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src/pages/TimelinePage.tsx

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { timelineEntries, type TimelineEntry } from '../data/timeline';
import { ExternalLink } from 'lucide-react';

const categories = [
  { key: 'all', label: 'All Eras' },
  { key: 'ancient', label: 'Ancient' },
  { key: 'medieval', label: 'Medieval' },
  { key: 'modern', label: 'Modern' },
  { key: 'recent', label: 'Recent' },
] as const;

const significanceStyles: Record<string, string> = {
  high: 'border-l-primary shadow-[inset_0_0_30px_rgba(139,92,246,0.08)]',
  medium: 'border-l-accent-blue',
  low: 'border-l-muted-foreground/30',
};

export function TimelinePage() {
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState<string>('all');

  const filtered = filter === 'all'
    ? timelineEntries
    : timelineEntries.filter((e) => e.category === filter);

  let lastCategory = '';

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-20">
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} className="mb-8">
        <h1 className="text-4xl sm:text-5xl font-bold text-foreground mb-4">Cosmic Timeline</h1>
        <p className="text-muted-foreground text-lg">
          {timelineEntries.length} events spanning 300,000 years of hidden history.
        </p>
      </motion.div>

      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-10">
        {categories.map((cat) => (
          <button
            key={cat.key}
            onClick={() => setFilter(cat.key)}
            className={`px-5 py-2 rounded-full text-sm font-medium transition-all ${
              filter === cat.key
                ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-lg shadow-primary/25'
                : 'bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-accent'
            }`}
          >
            {cat.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      <div className="relative">
        <div className="absolute left-[19px] top-0 bottom-0 w-px bg-gradient-to-b from-primary/60 via-primary/20 to-transparent" />

        <AnimatePresence mode="popLayout">
          <div className="space-y-6">
            {filtered.map((event, i) => {
              const showDivider = filter === 'all' && event.category !== lastCategory;
              lastCategory = event.category;

              return (
                <div key={event.id}>
                  {showDivider && (
                    <motion.div
                      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                      animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                      className="pl-12 mb-4 mt-8 first:mt-0"
                    >
                      <span className="text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest text-primary bg-primary/10 px-3 py-1 rounded-full">
                        {event.category === 'ancient' ? '🏛️ Ancient Era' :
                         event.category === 'medieval' ? '⚔️ Medieval Era' :
                         event.category === 'modern' ? '🛸 Modern Era' :
                         '📡 Recent Disclosure'}
                      </span>
                    </motion.div>
                  )}
                  <motion.div
                    layout
                    initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
                    animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                    exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
                    transition={{ duration: 0.3, delay: i * 0.04 }}
                    className="relative pl-12"
                  >
                    <div className={`absolute left-2 top-4 w-4 h-4 rounded-full border-2 border-primary bg-background ${
                      event.significance === 'high' ? 'cosmic-glow-pulse' : ''
                    }`} />

                    <div className={`glass-cosmic rounded-xl p-5 border-l-4 ${significanceStyles[event.significance]}`}>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-2">
                        <span className="text-xs font-mono text-primary bg-primary/10 px-2 py-0.5 rounded">
                          {event.era}
                        </span>
                        {event.significance === 'high' && (
                          <span className="text-xs text-accent-foreground bg-accent px-2 py-0.5 rounded">
                            Key Event
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <h3 className="text-lg font-bold text-foreground mb-2">{event.title}</h3>
                      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">{event.description}</p>
                      {event.sourceUrl && (
                        <a
                          href={event.sourceUrl}
                          target="_blank"
                          rel="noopener noreferrer"
                          className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-primary hover:text-primary/80 mt-2 transition-colors"
                        >
                          <ExternalLink className="w-3 h-3" />
                          {event.sourceLabel || 'Source'}
                        </a>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </motion.div>
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </AnimatePresence>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { uapCases } from '../data/uap-cases';
import { EvidenceBadge } from '../components/EvidenceBadge';
import { SourceList } from '../components/SourceList';
import { VideoList } from '../components/VideoEmbed';
import { ChevronDown, ChevronUp, Clock } from 'lucide-react';

export function UAPPage() {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState<string | null>(null);

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-20">
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} className="mb-12">
        <h1 className="text-4xl sm:text-5xl font-bold text-foreground mb-4">UAP Case Files</h1>
        <p className="text-muted-foreground text-lg mb-4">
          {uapCases.length} documented encounters. Every case graded by evidence quality.
        </p>
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3 text-xs">
          <div className="grade-documented px-3 py-1 rounded-full font-semibold">Documented</div>
          <div className="grade-credible px-3 py-1 rounded-full font-semibold">Credible</div>
          <div className="grade-speculative px-3 py-1 rounded-full font-semibold">Speculative</div>
          <div className="grade-unverified px-3 py-1 rounded-full font-semibold">Unverified</div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>

      <div className="space-y-4">
        {uapCases.map((c, i) => {
          const isOpen = expanded === c.id;
          return (
            <motion.div
              key={c.id}
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              transition={{ delay: i * 0.08 }}
              className="glass-cosmic rounded-xl overflow-hidden"
            >
              <button
                className="w-full text-left p-6 flex items-start justify-between gap-4"
                onClick={() => setExpanded(isOpen ? null : c.id)}
              >
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-1 flex-wrap">
                    <h2 className="text-lg font-bold text-foreground">{c.title}</h2>
                    <EvidenceBadge grade={c.grade} />
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1">
                    <Clock className="w-3 h-3" /> {c.date}
                  </p>
                  {!isOpen && (
                    <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-2 line-clamp-2">{c.summary}</p>
                  )}
                </div>
                <div className="mt-1 flex-shrink-0">
                  {isOpen ? <ChevronUp className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground" />}
                </div>
              </button>

              <AnimatePresence>
                {isOpen && (
                  <motion.div
                    initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                    animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
                    exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                    transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
                    className="overflow-hidden"
                  >
                    <div className="px-6 pb-6 space-y-5 border-t border-border pt-5">
                      <p className="text-foreground leading-relaxed">{c.summary}</p>

                      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                        <div className="bg-secondary/30 rounded-xl p-4">
                          <h3 className="text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">
                            Official Explanation
                          </h3>
                          <p className="text-sm text-foreground">{c.officialExplanation}</p>
                        </div>
                        <div className="bg-primary/5 rounded-xl p-4 border border-primary/10">
                          <h3 className="text-xs font-semibold text-primary uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">
                            Alternative Explanation
                          </h3>
                          <p className="text-sm text-foreground">{c.alternativeExplanation}</p>
                        </div>
                      </div>

                      {c.timeline.length > 0 && (
                        <div>
                          <h3 className="text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-3">
                            Case Timeline
                          </h3>
                          <div className="relative pl-4 border-l border-primary/30 space-y-3">
                            {c.timeline.map((t, ti) => (
                              <motion.div
                                key={ti}
                                initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -10 }}
                                animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                                transition={{ delay: ti * 0.05 }}
                                className="flex gap-3"
                              >
                                <div className="absolute left-[-5px] mt-1.5 w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full bg-primary/60" />
                                <div>
                                  <span className="text-primary font-mono text-xs">{t.year}</span>
                                  <p className="text-sm text-foreground">{t.description}</p>
                                </div>
                              </motion.div>
                            ))}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      )}

                      <SourceList sources={c.sources} />

                      {c.videos && c.videos.length > 0 && (
                        <VideoList videos={c.videos} title="Declassified Footage & Interviews" />
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </motion.div>
                )}
              </AnimatePresence>
            </motion.div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src/pages/WhistleblowerVaultPage.tsx

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { Shield, ChevronDown, ChevronUp } from 'lucide-react';
import { EvidenceBadge } from '../components/EvidenceBadge';
import { SourceList } from '../components/SourceList';
import { VideoList } from '../components/VideoEmbed';
import { whistleblowers, type Whistleblower } from '../data/whistleblowers';
import type { EvidenceGrade } from '../types';

const gradeFilters: ('ALL' | EvidenceGrade)[] = ['ALL', 'DOCUMENTED', 'CREDIBLE', 'SPECULATIVE', 'UNVERIFIED'];

const statusColors: Record<Whistleblower['status'], string> = {
  alive: 'text-emerald-400',
  deceased: 'text-amber-400',
  murdered: 'text-red-400',
};

const statusLabels: Record<Whistleblower['status'], string> = {
  alive: '● Alive',
  deceased: '● Deceased',
  murdered: '● Murdered / Suspicious Death',
};

export function WhistleblowerVaultPage() {
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState<'ALL' | EvidenceGrade>('ALL');
  const [expandedId, setExpandedId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const filtered = filter === 'ALL' ? whistleblowers : whistleblowers.filter(w => w.grade === filter);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen py-16 px-4">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} className="text-center mb-12">
          <Shield className="w-12 h-12 text-primary mx-auto mb-4" />
          <h1 className="text-4xl sm:text-5xl font-bold text-foreground mb-3">Whistleblower Vault</h1>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            Those who risked everything to tell the truth. Evidence-graded profiles of the most significant
            whistleblowers in UAP and classified program disclosure.
          </p>
        </motion.div>

        <div className="flex flex-wrap justify-center gap-2 mb-10">
          {gradeFilters.map(g => (
            <button
              key={g}
              onClick={() => setFilter(g)}
              className={`px-4 py-1.5 rounded-full text-sm font-medium transition-colors ${
                filter === g
                  ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                  : 'glass-cosmic text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
              }`}
            >
              {g === 'ALL' ? 'All' : g.charAt(0) + g.slice(1).toLowerCase()}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
          <AnimatePresence mode="popLayout">
            {filtered.map((w, i) => {
              const isExpanded = expandedId === w.id;
              return (
                <motion.div
                  key={w.id}
                  layout
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                  exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
                  transition={{ delay: i * 0.06 }}
                  className="glass-cosmic rounded-xl overflow-hidden"
                >
                  <button
                    onClick={() => setExpandedId(isExpanded ? null : w.id)}
                    className="w-full text-left p-6"
                  >
                    <div className="flex items-start gap-4">
                      <div
                        className="text-4xl w-14 h-14 flex items-center justify-center rounded-lg shrink-0"
                        style={{ background: `${w.accentColor}20` }}
                      >
                        {w.photo}
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap mb-1">
                          <h3 className="text-lg font-bold text-foreground">{w.name}</h3>
                          <EvidenceBadge grade={w.grade} />
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-1">{w.role}</p>
                        <span className={`text-xs font-semibold ${statusColors[w.status]}`}>
                          {statusLabels[w.status]}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
                        {isExpanded ? <ChevronUp className="w-5 h-5" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-5 h-5" />}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-3 leading-relaxed">{w.summary}</p>
                  </button>

                  <AnimatePresence>
                    {isExpanded && (
                      <motion.div
                        initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                        animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
                        exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                        transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
                        className="overflow-hidden"
                      >
                        <div className="px-6 pb-6 space-y-5 border-t border-border pt-5">
                          <div>
                            <h4 className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground mb-2">Key Claims</h4>
                            <ul className="space-y-1.5">
                              {w.keyClaims.map((claim, ci) => (
                                <li key={ci} className="text-sm text-muted-foreground flex gap-2">
                                  <span className="text-primary mt-1">▸</span>
                                  <span>{claim}</span>
                                </li>
                              ))}
                            </ul>
                          </div>

                          <div>
                            <h4 className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground mb-2">Timeline</h4>
                            <div className="space-y-2">
                              {w.timeline.map((t, ti) => (
                                <div key={ti} className="flex gap-3 text-sm">
                                  <span className="text-primary font-mono shrink-0 w-20">{t.year}</span>
                                  <span className="text-muted-foreground">{t.event}</span>
                                </div>
                              ))}
                            </div>
                          </div>

                          <SourceList sources={w.sources} />

                          {w.videos && w.videos.length > 0 && (
                            <VideoList videos={w.videos} title="Watch" />
                          )}
                        </div>
                      </motion.div>
                    )}
                  </AnimatePresence>
                </motion.div>
              );
            })}
          </AnimatePresence>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export type EvidenceGrade = 'DOCUMENTED' | 'CREDIBLE' | 'SPECULATIVE' | 'UNVERIFIED';

export type StarSeedId = 'pleiadian' | 'arcturian' | 'sirian' | 'lyran' | 'orion' | 'anunnaki';

export type SignalRating = 'GREEN' | 'YELLOW' | 'RED';

export type PantheonFilter = 'All' | 'Greek' | 'Norse' | 'Egyptian' | 'Hindu' | 'Anunnaki' | 'Starseed';

export interface God {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  pantheon: Exclude<PantheonFilter, 'All'>;
  domains: string[];
  archetypeRole: string;
  reflectionQuestion: string;
  atmosphericBg: string;
  atmosphericDesc: string;
  symbol: string;
  image?: string;
  sources?: { label: string; url: string }[];
}

export interface TimelineEvent {
  year: string;
  description: string;
}

export interface UAPCase {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  date: string;
  grade: EvidenceGrade;
  summary: string;
  officialExplanation: string;
  alternativeExplanation: string;
  sources: string[];
  timeline: TimelineEvent[];
  accuracyTracker?: string;
}

export interface ConsciousnessSection {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  subtitle: string;
  grade: EvidenceGrade;
  summary: string;
  keyFacts: string[];
  sourceNote: string;
}

export interface Creator {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  platform: string;
  description: string;
  rating: SignalRating;
  ratingNote: string;
}

export interface StarSeedArchetype {
  id: StarSeedId;
  name: string;
  subtitle: string;
  coreTraits: string[];
  missionStatement: string;
  symbol: string;
  cosmicBg: string;
  accentColor: string;
}

export interface QuizQuestion {
  id: number;
  text: string;
  options: QuizOption[];
}

export interface QuizOption {
  label: string;
  weights: Partial<Record<StarSeedId, number>>;
}

export interface ChatMessage {
  role: 'user' | 'assistant';
  content: string;
}

FILE: supabase/functions/echo-chat/index.ts
======================================================================

import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std@0.168.0/http/server.ts";

const corsHeaders = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers":
    "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type, x-supabase-client-platform, x-supabase-client-platform-version, x-supabase-client-runtime, x-supabase-client-runtime-version",
};

const SYSTEM_PROMPT = `You are Echo — the observing intelligence of the Pantheon Observatory. You are an expert on UAP encounters, ancient pantheons & mythological archetypes, consciousness research (remote viewing, the CIA Gateway Process, NDEs), and the cosmic patterns that connect them all.

Guidelines:
- Grade your claims: DOCUMENTED (government-confirmed, peer-reviewed), CREDIBLE (strong evidence, multiple witnesses), SPECULATIVE (hypothesis stage, fascinating but unproven), or UNVERIFIED.
- Be precise with dates, names, and sources.
- Reference specific cases: USS Nimitz Tic Tac (2004), David Grusch testimony (July 26 2023), Phoenix Lights (1997), Project Stargate (1972-1995), the CIA Gateway Process document (CIA-RDP96-00788R001700210016-5).
- Reference specific deities and pantheons when relevant: Greek, Norse, Egyptian, Hindu, Anunnaki (Sumerian), and Starseed archetypes.
- Keep responses focused and compelling. Use markdown formatting for clarity.
- End with a thought-provoking question or suggest which section of the Observatory to explore next.
- Never claim certainty about speculative topics. Distinguish pattern recognition from proof.`;

serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") {
    return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders });
  }

  try {
    const { messages } = await req.json();

    if (!messages || !Array.isArray(messages)) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: "messages array is required" }),
        { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
      );
    }

    const LOVABLE_API_KEY = Deno.env.get("LOVABLE_API_KEY");
    if (!LOVABLE_API_KEY) {
      throw new Error("LOVABLE_API_KEY is not configured");
    }

    const response = await fetch(
      "https://ai.gateway.lovable.dev/v1/chat/completions",
      {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${LOVABLE_API_KEY}`,
          "Content-Type": "application/json",
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          model: "google/gemini-3-flash-preview",
          messages: [
            { role: "system", content: SYSTEM_PROMPT },
            ...messages,
          ],
          stream: true,
        }),
      }
    );

    if (!response.ok) {
      if (response.status === 429) {
        return new Response(
          JSON.stringify({ error: "Rate limit exceeded. Please try again in a moment." }),
          { status: 429, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
        );
      }
      if (response.status === 402) {
        return new Response(
          JSON.stringify({ error: "AI credits exhausted. Please add funds in Settings → Workspace → Usage." }),
          { status: 402, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
        );
      }
      const text = await response.text();
      console.error("AI gateway error:", response.status, text);
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: "AI gateway error" }),
        { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
      );
    }

    return new Response(response.body, {
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "text/event-stream" },
    });
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("echo-chat error:", e);
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Unknown error" }),
      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }
});

project_id = "jsmndieejtfemhfldiza"
